            FROM servus_products

            LEFT OUTER JOIN servus_href
                ON servus_href.content_id = servus_products.id and servus_href.type = 'product'

                ON h1.content_id = servus_products.product_category_id and h1.type = 'product_category'
            LEFT OUTER JOIN servus_href h2
                ON h2.content_id = servus_products.product_subcategory_id and h2.type = 'product_category'

            FROM servus_products
